  var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
  xhr.open('POST', '/shop-assets/proxy/errorlog', true);
  xhr.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/json');
  xhr.send(JSON.stringify(payload));
}
function JSErrorLogger(){
  var self = this;
  self.handler = function(evt) {
    var obj = {
      "time": new Date().getTime(),
      "event": {
        "message": {
          "error-msg": evt.message,
          "error-file": evt.filename,
          "error-line": evt.lineno,
          "error-col": evt.colno,
          "JSESSIONID": (document.cookie.match(/(?:^|[; ])JSESSIONID=([^;]+)/) || '')[1],
          "AUTH_LOGIN": (document.cookie.match(/(?:^|[; ])AUTH_LOGIN=([^;]+)/) || '')[1],
          "SCC_COOKIE": (document.cookie.match(/(?:^|[; ])SCC_COOKIE=([^;]+)/) || '')[1],
          "user-agent": navigator.userAgent,
          "page-name": window.bb_pagegroup || 'unknown',
          "page-url": window.location.href
        },
        "severity": "info"
      }
    };
    // Do not call on production
    if (window.location.hostname !== 'www.cvs.com') {
      postErrorLog(obj);
    }
    return true;
  };
  self.JSErrorLogger = function() { window.addEventListener('error', self.handler); }();
}
